I gave one bottle to my children, and I opened the other one, but I didn't drink much. When I was about to check out, I discovered that the bottle of pure water I had not finished drinking was turbid and gray in color, with flocculent suspended matter after shaking. So I communicated with the hotel and asked them to send me a third-party test because I didn't feel any discomfort and I had to take a Yangtze River cruise in a hurry. I didn't go to the hospital for a checkup. I made it clear to the hotel staff at the time that I was traveling with my children and had no intention of causing trouble to them, but I needed to know what was contaminating the pure water. After the store promised to do third-party testing, my family and I left the store. I took a Yangtze River cruise ship from Yichang to Chongqing and returned to Yantai after four days of sightseeing in Chongqing. During this period, the hotel not only gave me a sample inspection result issued by Jingtian the next day, but also informed me that the water sample submitted for inspection was misconstrued by the cleaning staff of the manufacturer. The sewage was dumped. There has been no contact since. What I want to say here is that the hotel has been emphasizing to me that no matter if I call the police or make a complaint, they will actively cooperate and appear to be extremely sincere. However, when I left the hotel, I asked the hotel to send contaminated water samples to a third party for testing, instead of asking them to contact the manufacturer for testing. In this regard, the hotel is shirking its responsibility and did not fulfill its promise to me.
In terms of facilities and environment, Baogeli has done quite well, and the health service is a matter of opinion.
Personally, I don‚Äôt recommend a hotel that treats customers perfunctorily, because there are problems with its management. When there are no problems, everything is good, but when there are problems, it depends on who is unlucky, such as me.
